async def changeIcons():
    await bot.wait_until_ready()
    while not bot.is_closed:
        fp = open("Icons/" + random.choice(os.listdir("Icons")), 'rb')
        NewAvatar = fp.read()
        await bot.edit_profile(avatar = NewAvatar)
        await asyncio.sleep(600)```
